<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user, a senior ERP system architect, is building a cloud-based web ERP. The initial goal was to build out core ERP functionalities. During this session, the user requested two major new features:

1.  **Product Variations:** Implement a system to handle product variations (e.g., color, size) that are synced from WooCommerce. This required modifying the product catalog, purchase orders (PO), and goods received notes (GRN) to operate at the variation level for inventory tracking, while still presenting a single parent product on the storefront. The user also requested the ability to create new variable products with their variations directly from the ERP and have them sync to WooCommerce.
2.  **Manufacturing Module:** Build a new module to manage the manufacturing process. The user specified a workflow including:
    *   Management of Raw Materials (separate from finished products).
    *   Creation of a Bill of Materials (BOM) to define product recipes.
    *   A Work Order system to manage production runs.
    *   Integration with the financial system to track costs.
    *   A Manufacturing Dashboard with key performance indicators (KPIs).

**User's preferred language**: English

**what currently exists?**
The application is a full-stack ERP system with a FastAPI backend, React frontend, and MongoDB database.

In this session, two major features were added:
1.  **Product Variations:** The system now fully supports product variations. It can sync variations from WooCommerce, allows selecting specific variations in Purchase Orders and GRNs, and updates WooCommerce stock at the variation level. A UI was built within the ERP to create new variable products and their variations, which then sync to WooCommerce. The creation dialog can pull existing attributes (like 'Color', 'Size') directly from WooCommerce.
2.  **Manufacturing Module (Foundation):** The foundational structure for a manufacturing module has been built. This includes dedicated sections and backend logic for:
    *   **Raw Materials:** A separate inventory for manufacturing components.
    *   **Bill of Materials (BOM):** To define the raw materials required to produce a finished good.
    *   **Work Orders:** To track production jobs.
    *   These features are accessible via a new Manufacturing section in the main navigation.

**Key Technical Concepts**
-   **Product Variation Management:** Deep integration of a variation layer () into product, purchasing, and inventory models to track stock for specific product variants.
-   **External Configuration for UI:** Fetching attributes and terms from the external WooCommerce API to dynamically build the Create Variable Product form in the frontend, providing a better user experience.
-   **Module Scaffolding:** Building out the foundational API endpoints, database models, and placeholder UI pages for a major new feature (Manufacturing) in a structured way.
-   **Automated Testing of Workflows:** Using the  to simulate a multi-step user process (the full manufacturing cycle) to validate correctness.
